## addShippingMethodToCartWorkflow

This workflow adds shipping methods to a cart.

### Steps

### Hooks

#### cartCreated

##### Example

```ts
import { createCartWorkflow } from "@medusajs/medusa/core-flows"

createCartWorkflow.hooks.cartCreated(

		//TODO
	})
)
```

## validateExistingPaymentCollectionStep

This step validates that a cart doesn't have a payment collection.

## updateTaxLinesWorkflow

This workflow updates a cart's tax lines.

### Steps

<WorkflowDiagram workflow={{"name":"updateTaxLinesWorkflow","steps":[{"type":"step","name":"useRemoteQueryStep","description":"This step fetches data across modules using the remote query.\n\nLearn more in the [Remote Query documentation](https://docs.medusajs.com/advanced-development/modules/remote-query).\n\n","link":"../../core_flows.Steps_Common/page.mdx#useremotequerystep","depth":1},{"type":"step","name":"getItemTaxLinesStep","description":"This step retrieves the tax lines of the specified line items in a cart.","link":"../../core_flows.Steps_Cart/page.mdx#getitemtaxlinesstep","depth":2},{"type":"step","name":"setTaxLinesForItemsStep","description":"This step sets the tax lines of shipping methods and line items in a cart.","link":"../../core_flows.Steps_Cart/page.mdx#settaxlinesforitemsstep","depth":3}]}} />
